GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_f*A**c2
Candidate formulas: 80

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
0.5229500625821207\,A^{1/3}-0.3254156367450257\,\sqrt{A}.
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have no residual \(t\)-dependence after parameter choice, (ii) have no extra constant offset term, and (iii) reduce exactly to a linear combination of \(A^{1/3}\) and \(\sqrt{A}\) with the above coefficients.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all non-\(A^{1/3}\) and non-\(\sqrt{A}\) terms can be eliminated by setting some candidate constants to 0 (or otherwise making them identically constant), and then whether the remaining coefficients can be set to the GT values.

You can set \(c0=0,c3=0,c4=0\) leaving one power only. **No match**.
